t-bullets--no-spacing" data-test=3D"darwin-journal-homepage-promo-text"> <p>The journal=E2=80=99s ultimate goal is to provide the mi= crobiology community with an open access mid-level impact journal for quali= ty research encompassing all aspects of environmental microbiology=E2=80=94= from air, to soil, to water, and beyond. The journal is committed to a posi= tive author experience with rapid turnaround time for submissions, thorough= and timely peer review, aided by Editors working across <em>Microbiome</em= > and <em>Environmental Microbiome</em>. Publications in <em= >Environmental Microbiome</em> should aim to have an applied context that w= ill shape future innovation and research by connecting genomic and microbio= me analyses to their
